about /əˈbaʊt/	关于；大约；到处<br>prep.; adv. | A1<br>We talked about our weekend plans after lunch.<br>午饭后我们聊了周末的计划。<br>talk about;about time;think about<br>about 可记成 a + bout：绕着一件事转一圈。
above /əˈbʌv/	在……上面；高于<br>prep.; adv. | A1<br>The clock hangs above the classroom door.<br>时钟挂在教室门的上方。<br>above average;above all;rise above<br>a-bove：把 bove 想成“高处的位置”。
across /əˈkrɒs/	穿过；在对面<br>prep.; adv. | A1<br>She walked across the quiet street carefully.<br>她小心地走过那条安静的街道。<br>across the road;come across;walk across<br>across = a + cross，像从十字路口穿过去。
act /ækt/	行动；表演；行为<br>verb; noun | A1<br>Please act quickly if you hear the alarm.<br>若听到警报，请迅速行动。<br>act quickly;act as;in the act<br>act 很短，像舞台上一声令下就开始演。
activity /ækˈtɪvəti/	活动；行动<br>noun | A1<br>The school plans a new outdoor activity this Friday.<br>学校计划本周五开展新的户外活动。<br>outdoor activity;after-school activity;group activity<br>activity 来自 active：保持活跃就会有活动。
actor /ˈæktə(r)/	男演员；演员<br>noun | A1<br>He wants to become a film actor one day.<br>他希望有一天成为电影演员。<br>film actor;lead actor;become an actor<br>actor = act + or，做表演动作的人。
add /æd/	添加；增加<br>verb | A1<br>Please add a little sugar to my tea.<br>请往我的茶里加点糖。<br>add sugar;add up;add to<br>add 像往杯子里再倒一点进去。
address /əˈdres/	地址；演说；处理<br>noun; verb | A1<br>Please write your home address on this form.<br>请在这张表格上填写家庭住址。<br>home address;email address;address a problem<br>address 可记：寄信一定要写对地址。
adult /ˈædʌlt/	成年人；成年的<br>noun; adj. | A1<br>Only an adult can buy the cinema tickets tonight.<br>今晚只有成年人可以买电影院的票。<br>young adult;adult ticket;adult life<br>adult 与 child 相对，想到“长大了”。
afraid /əˈfreɪd/	害怕的；担心的<br>adj. | A1<br>The little boy is afraid of the dark room.<br>小男孩害怕那间黑暗的房间。<br>afraid of;be afraid;feel afraid<br>a-fraid：心里发“fra”抖的感觉。
after /ˈɑːftə(r)/	在……之后<br>prep.; conj.; adv. | A1<br>We usually play football after school.<br>我们通常放学后踢足球。<br>after school;after that;look after<br>after 和 afternoon 同源：午后就是 after noon。
afternoon /ˌɑːftəˈnuːn/	下午<br>noun | A1<br>Shall we meet this afternoon at the library?<br>我们今天下午在图书馆见面好吗？<br>this afternoon;in the afternoon;good afternoon<br>after + noon：中午之后就是下午。
again /əˈɡen/	再一次；又<br>adv. | A1<br>Could you say that again more slowly?<br>你能再说一遍、慢一点吗？<br>try again;once again;come again<br>again 像回声，事情又来一遍。
age /eɪdʒ/	年龄；时代<br>noun | A1<br>She started piano lessons at the age of six.<br>她六岁开始学钢琴。<br>at the age of;old age;age group<br>age 很短，记住“几岁”就是 age。
ago /əˈɡəʊ/	以前<br>adv. | A1<br>I met her at a party two years ago.<br>两年前我在一次聚会上遇见她。<br>years ago;long ago;a week ago<br>a-go：时间已经走远了。
agree /əˈɡriː/	同意；达成一致<br>verb | A1<br>I agree with your idea about the trip.<br>我同意你关于这次旅行的想法。<br>agree with;agree to;agree on<br>agree 里有 gree，像 green 一样“谈妥了很顺”。
air /eə(r)/	空气；空中<br>noun | A1<br>Let's open the window for some fresh air.<br>我们开窗透透新鲜空气吧。<br>fresh air;by air;in the air<br>air 读起来轻飘飘，像空气。
airport /ˈeəpɔːt/	机场<br>noun | A1<br>We will meet you at the airport tomorrow morning.<br>我们明天早上在机场接你。<br>at the airport;airport taxi;international airport<br>air + port：空中的港口就是机场。
all /ɔːl/	全部；所有<br>det.; pron.; adv. | A1<br>They spent all day cleaning the flat.<br>他们花了一整天打扫公寓。<br>all day;all of;above all<br>all 开口很大，像把一切都包进去。
almost /ˈɔːlməʊst/	几乎；差不多<br>adv. | A1<br>Dinner is almost ready, so please wash your hands.<br>晚饭差不多好了，请去洗手。<br>almost ready;almost always;almost there<br>almost = all + most：还差一点点就全部。
alone /əˈləʊn/	独自的；单独地<br>adj.; adv. | A1<br>She prefers to study alone in the quiet room.<br>她更喜欢在安静的房间里独自学习。<br>live alone;leave alone;feel alone<br>alone 与 along 易混：alone 是一个人。
along /əˈlɒŋ/	沿着；一起<br>prep.; adv. | A1<br>We walked along the river after dinner.<br>晚饭后我们沿着河边散步。<br>along the river;come along;walk along<br>a-long：顺着一条长线往前走。
already /ɔːlˈredi/	已经<br>adv. | A1<br>I have already finished my homework today.<br>我今天已经做完作业了。<br>already know;already done;have already<br>al-ready：已经准备好了。
also /ˈɔːlsəʊ/	也；同样<br>adv. | A1<br>She can also speak a little French.<br>她也会说一点法语。<br>also like;not only...also;can also<br>also 放句中，表示“另外还有”。
always /ˈɔːlweɪz/	总是；永远<br>adv. | A1<br>He always drinks coffee in the morning.<br>他早上总是喝咖啡。<br>always late;always remember;almost always<br>all + ways：所有路上都会发生。
and /ænd/	和；并且<br>conj. | A1<br>Please buy bread and milk on your way home.<br>回家路上请买面包和牛奶。<br>bread and butter;and then;come and see<br>and 像连接两节火车车厢。
angry /ˈæŋɡri/	生气的<br>adj. | A1<br>Don't get angry with him about the mistake.<br>别为这个错误对他生气。<br>angry with;get angry;angry about<br>angry 发音里有 ang，像心里拧着。
animal /ˈænɪml/	动物<br>noun | A1<br>The children love looking at farm animals.<br>孩子们喜欢看农场里的动物。<br>wild animal;farm animal;animal hospital<br>animal 可拆成 ani-mal，想到活物。
another /əˈnʌðə(r)/	另一个；再一<br>det.; pron. | A1<br>Could I have another cup of tea, please?<br>请再给我一杯茶好吗？<br>another day;one another;another one<br>an + other：另外一个 other。
answer /ˈɑːnsə(r)/	答案；回答<br>noun; verb | A1<br>Please answer the phone when it rings.<br>电话铃响时请接一下。<br>answer the phone;give an answer;correct answer<br>answer 对 question：问完就要答。
any /ˈeni/	任何；一些（否定/疑问）<br>det.; pron.; adv. | A1<br>Do you have any questions about the lesson?<br>关于这节课你有什么问题吗？<br>any questions;anyone;not any<br>any 在问句里常表“有没有一些”。
anyone /ˈeniwʌn/	任何人<br>pron. | A1<br>Anyone can join the club after school.<br>放学后任何人都可以加入这个俱乐部。<br>anyone else;anyone can;if anyone<br>any + one：任意某一个人。
anything /ˈeniθɪŋ/	任何事物<br>pron. | A1<br>Is there anything else you need from the shop?<br>你还需要从店里买别的东西吗？<br>anything else;not anything;say anything<br>any + thing：任意一件东西。
apple /ˈæpl/	苹果<br>noun | A1<br>She packed a red apple in her lunch box.<br>她在午餐盒里放了一个红苹果。<br>red apple;apple juice;apple pie<br>apple 很常见，想到苹果手机也容易记。
April /ˈeɪprəl/	四月<br>noun | A1<br>Her birthday is in early April this year.<br>她今年的生日在四月初。<br>in April;early April;April weather<br>A-pril：春天四月的 A 开头月份。
area /ˈeəriə/	地区；面积；领域<br>noun | A1<br>There is a new park in our local area.<br>我们本地新开了一座公园。<br>local area;play area;in the area<br>area 像一片开阔地带。
arm /ɑːm/	手臂；扶手<br>noun | A1<br>He hurt his left arm during the football match.<br>他在足球比赛中伤了左臂。<br>left arm;arm in arm;break an arm<br>arm 短，抬起手臂就能感觉到。
around /əˈraʊnd/	周围；大约<br>adv.; prep. | A1<br>We walked around the city for two hours.<br>我们在城里转了两个小时。<br>look around;around the city;around six<br>a-round：绕着圆圈走。
arrive /əˈraɪv/	到达<br>verb | A1<br>The train will arrive at the station at noon.<br>火车将在中午到达车站。<br>arrive at;arrive in;arrive home<br>arrive 与 leave 相对：到站 vs 离站。
art /ɑːt/	艺术；美术<br>noun | A1<br>She takes an art class every Wednesday.<br>她每周三上美术课。<br>art class;modern art;work of art<br>art 短而响亮，像画室里的一声。
ask /ɑːsk/	问；请求<br>verb | A1<br>You can ask the teacher if you need help.<br>需要帮助时可以问老师。<br>ask a question;ask for;ask about<br>ask 嘴一张就发出请求。
at /æt/	在；朝；以<br>prep. | A1<br>I usually have breakfast at home.<br>我通常在家吃早餐。<br>at home;at school;look at<br>at 点状位置：在某一点。
August /ˈɔːɡəst/	八月<br>noun | A1<br>We usually travel in late August.<br>我们通常在八月下旬旅行。<br>in August;late August;August holiday<br>August 像夏天尾巴的月份。
aunt /ɑːnt/	姑妈；姨妈；婶婶<br>noun | A1<br>My aunt lives near the train station.<br>我姨妈住在火车站附近。<br>my aunt;aunt and uncle;visit my aunt<br>aunt 与 uncle 成对记。
autumn /ˈɔːtəm/	秋天（英式）<br>noun | A1<br>The leaves turn brown in autumn.<br>秋天树叶变成褐色。<br>in autumn;autumn leaves;autumn term<br>英式用 autumn，美式常说 fall。
away /əˈweɪ/	离开；不在<br>adv. | A1<br>Please put your books away after class.<br>下课后请把书收好。<br>go away;far away;put away<br>a-way：走向远处。
baby /ˈbeɪbi/	婴儿；宝贝<br>noun | A1<br>Their new baby sleeps most of the day.<br>他们的新生儿白天大多在睡觉。<br>new baby;baby brother;baby food<br>baby 叠音可爱，像哄孩子。
back /bæk/	背；后面；回来<br>noun; adv.; adj. | A1<br>Please come back before it gets dark.<br>请在天黑前回来。<br>come back;at the back;back door<br>back 既是背，也是往回走。
bad /bæd/	坏的；糟糕的<br>adj. | A1<br>We cancelled the picnic because of bad weather.<br>因为天气不好，我们取消了野餐。<br>bad news;bad weather;feel bad<br>bad 与 good 成对记。
bag /bæɡ/	包；袋子<br>noun | A1<br>She put the apples in a plastic bag.<br>她把苹果装进塑料袋。<br>school bag;plastic bag;bag of<br>bag 短促，像把东西装进去。
ball /bɔːl/	球<br>noun | A1<br>The children kicked a ball in the park.<br>孩子们在公园里踢球。<br>kick a ball;ball game;tennis ball<br>ball 圆圆的，发音也圆。
banana /bəˈnɑːnə/	香蕉<br>noun | A1<br>He eats a banana after morning exercise.<br>晨练后他会吃一根香蕉。<br>ripe banana;banana milkshake;eat a banana<br>ba-na-na 三个音节，像弯弯的香蕉。
band /bænd/	乐队；带子<br>noun | A1<br>Their school band will play at the festival.<br>他们的校乐队将在节日演出。<br>rock band;school band;wrist band<br>band 可记成一群人绑在一起演奏。
bank /bæŋk/	银行；岸<br>noun | A1<br>I need to go to the bank this afternoon.<br>我今天下午需要去银行。<br>bank account;river bank;at the bank<br>bank 存钱，也可指河岸。
bath /bɑːθ/	洗澡；浴缸<br>noun | A1<br>She likes to have a bath after a long day.<br>忙完漫长的一天后她喜欢洗个澡。<br>have a bath;bath time;run a bath<br>bath 英式常说 have a bath。
bathroom /ˈbɑːθruːm/	浴室；卫生间<br>noun | A1<br>The bathroom is at the end of the hall.<br>浴室在走廊尽头。<br>bathroom door;in the bathroom;shared bathroom<br>bath + room：洗澡的房间。
be /biː/	是；在；成为<br>verb | A1<br>Please be quiet during the exam.<br>考试时请保持安静。<br>be careful;be quiet;will be<br>be 是最基础的“是/在”。
beach /biːtʃ/	海滩<br>noun | A1<br>We spent the whole day at the sandy beach.<br>我们在沙滩上待了一整天。<br>sandy beach;at the beach;beach holiday<br>beach 有 ea，像海浪的声音。
beautiful /ˈbjuːtɪfl/	美丽的<br>adj. | A1<br>It is a beautiful day for a long walk.<br>今天适合好好散个步，天气真美。<br>beautiful day;beautiful view;look beautiful<br>beauty + ful：充满美。
because /bɪˈkɒz/	因为<br>conj. | A1<br>I stayed home because I felt tired.<br>我待在家里，因为我觉得累了。<br>because of;just because;because I<br>be-cause：事情的原因。
become /bɪˈkʌm/	变成；成为<br>verb | A1<br>She hopes to become a doctor in future.<br>她希望将来成为一名医生。<br>become a teacher;become angry;become clear<br>be + come：变成某种样子到来。

bedroom /ˈbedruːm/	卧室<br>noun | A1<br>His bedroom window looks onto the garden.<br>他卧室的窗户朝向花园。<br>my bedroom;bedroom window;shared bedroom<br>bed + room：放床的房间。
beer /bɪə(r)/	啤酒<br>noun | A1<br>He ordered a cold beer with his meal.<br>他点餐时要了一杯冰啤酒。<br>a glass of beer;cold beer;drink beer<br>beer 双 e，像泡沫升起。
before /bɪˈfɔː(r)/	在……之前<br>prep.; conj.; adv. | A1<br>Brush your teeth before you go to bed.<br>睡觉前请刷牙。<br>before school;the day before;before long<br>be-fore：站在时间前面。
begin /bɪˈɡɪn/	开始<br>verb | A1<br>The film will begin in ten minutes.<br>电影十分钟后开始。<br>begin with;begin to;begin work<br>begin 与 end 成对。
behind /bɪˈhaɪnd/	在……后面<br>prep.; adv. | A1<br>The cat is hiding behind the door.<br>猫藏在门后面。<br>behind the door;fall behind;leave behind<br>be-hind：在后边。
believe /bɪˈliːv/	相信；认为<br>verb | A1<br>I believe that we can finish this today.<br>我相信我们今天能完成这件事。<br>believe in;hard to believe;believe that<br>believe 里有 lie，但意思是相信而非撒谎——注意区分。
below /bɪˈləʊ/	在……下面；低于<br>prep.; adv. | A1<br>Temperatures may fall below zero tonight.<br>今晚气温可能降到零度以下。<br>below zero;see below;below average<br>be-low：位置偏低。
belt /belt/	腰带；地带<br>noun | A1<br>Please fasten your seat belt before we leave.<br>出发前请系好安全带。<br>seat belt;leather belt;green belt<br>belt 系在腰上，seat belt 系在座位上。
best /best/	最好的；最好地<br>adj.; adv.; noun | A1<br>She is my best friend at school.<br>她是我学校里最好的朋友。<br>best friend;do your best;the best<br>good → better → best。

bicycle /ˈbaɪsɪkl/	自行车<br>noun | A1<br>He rides a bicycle to school every day.<br>他每天骑自行车上学。<br>ride a bicycle;bicycle lane;by bicycle<br>bi + cycle：两个轮子转起来。

party /ˈpɑːti/	聚会；政党<br>noun | A2<br>They will throw a birthday party on Saturday.<br>他们周六要办一场生日聚会。<br>birthday party;political party;throw a party<br>party 一群人聚一起——要么狂欢，要么议政。

passenger /ˈpæsɪndʒə(r)/	乘客<br>noun | A2<br>The bus stopped to pick up more passengers.<br>公交车停下来接更多乘客。<br>train passenger;passenger seat;passenger list<br>pass + enger：一路“经过、搭乘”的人。
passport /ˈpɑːspɔːt/	护照<br>noun | A2<br>Do not forget your passport at the airport.<br>在机场别忘记带护照。<br>valid passport;passport control;apply for a passport<br>pass + port：过港口、过边境的通行证。
past /pɑːst/	过去的；经过<br>adj.; noun; prep. | A2<br>She walked past the old bookshop this morning.<br>她今天早上走过那家旧书店。<br>in the past;walk past;past tense<br>past 既是“从前”，也是从你身边“掠过”。
pasta /ˈpæstə/	意大利面<br>noun | A2<br>We cooked some tomato pasta for dinner tonight.<br>今晚我们做了番茄意面当晚饭。<br>fresh pasta;pasta sauce;cook pasta<br>pasta 音近“帕斯塔”，一锅热乎乎的意面。
path /pɑːθ/	小路；路径<br>noun | A2<br>Follow the garden path to the small gate.<br>沿着花园小径走到那扇小门。<br>garden path;follow the path;mountain path<br>path 窄窄一条，是脚一步步踩出来的路。
pay /peɪ/	支付；工资<br>verb; noun | A2<br>Can you pay the bill with your card?<br>你能用卡付这笔账吗？<br>pay the bill;pay attention;pay for<br>pay：钱从口袋“付”出去，那一声就叫 pay。
pen /pen/	钢笔；笔<br>noun | A2<br>Please sign your name with a blue pen.<br>请用蓝色钢笔签上你的名字。<br>blue pen;write with a pen;ballpoint pen<br>pen 细细一支，墨水流过就成了字。
pencil /ˈpensl/	铅笔<br>noun | A2<br>She wrote all her answers carefully in pencil.<br>她用铅笔仔细写完了所有答案。<br>sharp pencil;pencil case;write in pencil<br>pencil 写错能擦，考试时最放心的工具。
people /ˈpiːpl/	人们<br>noun | A2<br>Lots of young people meet in the city park.<br>很多年轻人在城市公园见面。<br>local people;young people;lots of people<br>people 是复数集合：别说 a people 指“一个人”。
pepper /ˈpepə(r)/	胡椒；柿子椒<br>noun | A2<br>Please pass the black pepper for my soup.<br>请把黑胡椒递给我放汤里。<br>black pepper;green pepper;salt and pepper<br>pepper 像“泼泼”撒一点，菜就香了。
per /pɜː(r)/	每<br>prep. | A2<br>Tickets cost twenty pounds per person at the door.<br>今天门票在门口每人二十英镑。<br>pounds per kilo;per person;per hour<br>per = 每一个：看价签常写 per kilo。
perfect /ˈpɜːfɪkt/	完美的<br>adj. | A2<br>The weather was perfect for a long morning walk.<br>天气非常适合清晨长时间散步。<br>perfect timing;perfect weather;look perfect<br>per-fect：做到头了，几乎挑不出毛病。
perhaps /pəˈhæps/	也许<br>adv. | A2<br>Perhaps we can visit the museum together tomorrow.<br>也许我们明天可以一起去博物馆。<br>perhaps later;perhaps not;or perhaps<br>per-haps：hap 想成 happen——也许会发生。
period /ˈpɪəriəd/	时期；句号<br>noun | A2<br>She stayed abroad for a short period last year.<br>她去年在国外待了一小段时间。<br>a short period;exam period;full period<br>period 句末那个点，也像一段时间画上句号。
person /ˈpɜːsn/	人<br>noun | A2<br>She is the right person for this difficult job.<br>她是这份困难工作的合适人选。<br>a young person;the right person;per person<br>person 指单个的人；people 多指一群。
personal /ˈpɜːsənl/	个人的<br>adj. | A2<br>Please keep all your personal details private online.<br>请在网上保护好你的全部个人资料。<br>personal life;personal opinion;personal details<br>personal = person + al：属于某个人的。
pet /pet/	宠物<br>noun | A2<br>Our family pet always sleeps beside the warm sofa.<br>我们家的宠物总爱睡在暖和的沙发旁。<br>keep a pet;family pet;pet dog<br>pet 又短又软，像摸宠物时轻声叫它。
petrol /ˈpetrəl/	汽油（英式）<br>noun | A2<br>We stopped at a petrol station near the town.<br>我们在镇附近的加油站停了下来。<br>petrol station;petrol price;fill up with petrol<br>petrol（英）= gasoline（美）：记英国加油站牌。
phone /fəʊn/	电话；打电话<br>noun; verb | A2<br>I will phone a friend after dinner tonight.<br>今晚晚饭后我给朋友打个电话。<br>mobile phone;on the phone;phone a friend<br>phone 可当名词也可当动词：直接 phone her。
photo /ˈfəʊtəʊ/	照片<br>noun | A2<br>She took a photo of the quiet blue lake.<br>她拍了一张安静蓝色湖面的照片。<br>take a photo;family photo;old photo<br>photo 是 photograph 的口语短版。

piano /piˈænəʊ/	钢琴<br>noun | A2<br>She has a piano lesson every Thursday morning.<br>她每周四上午有钢琴课。<br>play the piano;piano lesson;grand piano<br>piano 结尾像“噢”，琴声一响就想起它。

picture /ˈpɪktʃə(r)/	图片；图画<br>noun | A2<br>Can you draw a picture of your new house?<br>你能画一幅你新房子的图吗？<br>take a picture;draw a picture;in the picture<br>picture 里有 pict：像把画面 pict 出来。
piece /piːs/	一块；一件<br>noun | A2<br>Could I have one piece of cake after lunch?<br>午饭后可以给我一块蛋糕吗？<br>a piece of cake;piece of paper;one piece<br>piece 发音像 peace，切下一小块就平静了。
pig /pɪɡ/	猪<br>noun | A2<br>The farm pig rolled happily in the soft mud.<br>农场的猪开心地在软泥里打滚。<br>farm pig;roast pig;pig farm<br>pig 很短，像猪哼一声的口型。
pink /pɪŋk/	粉色的；粉色<br>adj.; noun | A2<br>She wore a bright pink dress to school today.<br>她今天穿了件亮粉色连衣裙去学校。<br>bright pink;pink dress;turn pink<br>pink 像花瓣“乒”地一下展开的粉。

purple /ˈpɜːpl/	紫色的<br>adj.; noun | A2<br>She chose a purple dress for the party tonight.<br>她为今晚的派对选了一条紫色连衣裙。<br>purple dress;dark purple;purple flowers<br>purple：红加蓝混出的颜色。
